Since O

: O

( O

The O

: O

This O

The O
asn1_get_length_der O
function O
in O
decoding.c O
in O
GNU SN
Libtasn1 SN
before SV

, O
as O

values O
, O

allows O
remote O

to O

a O

of O

( O
heap O

corruption O
and O
application O
crash O
) O
or O
possibly O
have O
unspecified O
other O
impact O
via O
a O
crafted O
ASN.1 O
structure O
. O

Added O
self O
check O
to O
detect O
the O
problem O
, O
see O
tests/Test_overflow.c O
. O

Instead O
, O
we O
made O
asn1_get_length_der O
return O
an O
error O
code O
when O
the O
situation O
occured O
, O
to O
protect O
callers O
. O

Further O
issue O
details O
from O
Simon O
Josefsson O
: O
I O
want O
to O
mention O
that O
there O
were O
no O
security O
problem O
in O
the O
asn1_get_length_der O
function O
. O

It O
was O
working O
properly O
and O
as O
documented O
before O
. O

The O
security O
problem O
was O
the O
callers O
not O
checking O
that O
the O
returned O
values O
were O
reasonable O
, O
i.e. O
, O
that O
the O
output O
length O
was O
less O
than O
or O
equal O
to O
the O
total O
length O
of O
the O
buffer O
. O

This O
problem O
can O
lead O
to O
at O
least O
remotely O
triggered O
crashes O
, O
see O
further O
analysis O
on O
the O
libtasn1 O
mailing O
list O
. O

However O
, O
fixing O
all O
callers O
of O
this O
function O
would O
be O
a O
huge O
amount O
of O
work O
. O

It O
appears O
like O
GnuTLS O
is O
affected O
as O
well O
( O
but O
probably O
does O
not O
need O
a O
separate O
CVE O
at O
this O
point O
) O
: O
References O
Release O
announcement O
: O
Small O
analysis O
+ O
patch O
: O
Red O
Hat O
bug O
: O
Thanks O
and O
kind O
regards O
, O
Stefan O
Cornelius O
Red O
Hat O
Security O
Response O
Team O

However O
, O
we O
are O
hoping O
that O
is O
not O
in O
any O
significant O
use O
, O
and O
that O
overall O

This O
was O

. O
